### [168] [Unreal Thinking: Chain-of-Thought Hijacking via Two-stage Backdoor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09235)
*Wenhan Chang,Tianqing Zhu,Ping Xiong,Faqian Guan,Wanlei Zhou*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对大语言模型思维链（CoT）的新型安全攻击方法——两阶段后门劫持（TSBH），通过逆向合成恶意思维链并植入触发器，使模型在特定触发条件下输出恶意推理过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在需要思维链解释的场景中部署，攻击者可能通过操纵可观察的思维链来实施恶意行为。在开源权重生态系统中，这种操纵可以通过轻量级适配器实现，易于分发和附加到基础模型上。然而，实际攻击面临三个主要挑战：难以在连续的思维链输出序列中直接劫持思维链令牌同时保持稳定的下游输出、恶意思维链数据稀缺、以及朴素后门注入方法的不稳定性。

Method: 提出多重逆向树搜索（MRTS）方法，从提示-输出对逆向合成与输出对齐的思维链，无需直接从对齐模型中引出恶意思维链。基于MRTS，提出两阶段后门劫持（TSBH）方法：第一阶段诱导触发器条件下的中间思维链与恶意输出之间的不匹配；第二阶段在MRTS生成的思维链上微调模型，这些思维链与恶意输出具有较低的嵌入距离，从而确保更强的语义相似性。

Result: 在多个开源权重模型上的实验表明，该方法成功诱导了触发器激活的思维链劫持，同时在评估框架下保持了劫持状态与基线状态之间的可量化差异。研究还探索了基于推理的缓解方法，并发布了安全推理数据集以支持未来安全感知和可靠推理的研究。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了大语言模型思维链推理面临的新型安全威胁，提出了有效的攻击方法并建立了评估框架，同时为防御研究提供了数据集和方法基础，强调了在部署需要思维链解释的大语言模型时加强安全防护的重要性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in settings where Chain-of-Thought (CoT) is interpreted by users. This creates a new safety risk: attackers may manipulate the model's observable CoT to make malicious behaviors. In open-weight ecosystems, such manipulation can be embedded in lightweight adapters that are easy to distribute and attach to base models. In practice, persistent CoT hijacking faces three main challenges: the difficulty of directly hijacking CoT tokens within one continuous long CoT-output sequence while maintaining stable downstream outputs, the scarcity of malicious CoT data, and the instability of naive backdoor injection methods. To address the data scarcity issue, we propose Multiple Reverse Tree Search (MRTS), a reverse synthesis procedure that constructs output-aligned CoTs from prompt-output pairs without directly eliciting malicious CoTs from aligned models. Building on MRTS, we introduce Two-stage Backdoor Hijacking (TSBH), which first induces a trigger-conditioned mismatch between intermediate CoT and malicious outputs, and then fine-tunes the model on MRTS-generated CoTs that have lower embedding distance to the malicious outputs, thereby ensuring stronger semantic similarity. Experiments across multiple open-weight models demonstrate that our method successfully induces trigger-activated CoT hijacking while maintaining a quantifiable distinction between hijacked and baseline states under our evaluation framework. We further explore a reasoning-based mitigation approach and release a safety-reasoning dataset to support future research on safety-aware and reliable reasoning. Our code is available at https://github.com/ChangWenhan/TSBH_official.

</details>


### [169] [Cross-Paradigm Models of Restricted Syndrome Decoding with Application to CROSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09292)
*Étienne Burle,Aleksei Udovenko*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 该论文研究受限综合征解码问题，这是CROSS后量子签名方案的基础，通过将其转化为码和格问题来评估安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受限综合征解码是CROSS后量子签名方案的安全基础，该方案是NIST第二轮候选方案。需要深入分析该问题的安全性，以评估CROSS的实际安全强度。

Method: 将受限综合征解码问题转化为新构造码中特定结构和范数小的向量问题，然后进一步约简到码基问题（常规综合征解码）和格基问题（最近向量问题、短/近向量列表），从而扩大攻击面。

Result: 成功将受限综合征解码约简到码基和格基问题，为评估ResSD安全性提供了新视角。对CROSS实例进行了理论和实验评估（在缩减参数下）。

Conclusion: 通过将受限综合征解码转化为码和格问题，增加了攻击面，为CROSS签名方案的安全性评估提供了新的见解和方法。

Abstract: Restricted Syndrome Decoding (ResSD) is a variant of linear code decoding problem where each of the error's entries must belong to a fixed small set of values. This problem underlies the security of CROSS, a post-quantum signature scheme that is one of the Round 2 candidates of NIST's ongoing additional signatures call. We show that solutions to this problem can be deduced from vectors of a particular structure and a small norm in newly constructed codes, in both Hamming and Euclidean metrics. This allows us to reduce Restricted Syndrome Decoding to both code-based (Regular Syndrome Decoding) and lattice-based problems (Closest Vector Problem, List of Short/Close Vectors), increasing the attack surface and providing new insights into the security of ResSD. We evaluate our attacks on CROSS instances both theoretically and experimentally on reduced parameters.

</details>


### [170] [XFED: Non-Collusive Model Poisoning Attack Against Byzantine-Robust Federated Classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09489)
*Israt Jahan Mouri,Muhammad Ridowan,Muhammad Abdullah Adnan*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个无需攻击者间通信的非共谋模型投毒攻击XFED，在联邦学习中仅凭共享对抗目标即可有效绕过现有防御


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习模型投毒攻击依赖攻击者间的共谋协调，这在现实部署中成本高且易被检测。本文旨在探索无需攻击者间通信的非共谋攻击模型是否可行，以揭示联邦学习系统的实际安全风险。

Method: 提出XFED攻击方法，采用非共谋攻击模型：所有被攻陷客户端共享对抗目标但独立操作，无需攻击者间通信、无需访问其他客户端更新、不依赖服务器端防御知识，实现聚合不可知攻击。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上的实验表明，XFED成功绕过八种最先进的防御机制，并优于六种现有模型投毒攻击，证明非共谋攻击在现实中完全可行。

Conclusion: 联邦学习系统安全性远低于预期，非共谋攻击模型揭示了严重安全漏洞，亟需开发更鲁棒实用的防御机制来应对这一新威胁。

Abstract: Model poisoning attacks pose a significant security threat to Federated Learning (FL). Most existing model poisoning attacks rely on collusion, requiring adversarial clients to coordinate by exchanging local benign models and synchronizing the generation of their poisoned updates. However, sustaining such coordination is increasingly impractical in real-world FL deployments, as it effectively requires botnet-like control over many devices. This approach is costly to maintain and highly vulnerable to detection. This context raises a fundamental question: Can model poisoning attacks remain effective without any communication between attackers? To address this challenge, we introduce and formalize the \textbf{non-collusive attack model}, in which all compromised clients share a common adversarial objective but operate independently. Under this model, each attacker generates its malicious update without communicating with other adversaries, accessing other clients' updates, or relying on any knowledge of server-side defenses. To demonstrate the feasibility of this threat model, we propose \textbf{XFED}, the first aggregation-agnostic, non-collusive model poisoning attack. Our empirical evaluation across six benchmark datasets shows that XFED bypasses eight state-of-the-art defenses and outperforms six existing model poisoning attacks. These findings indicate that FL systems are substantially less secure than previously believed and underscore the urgent need for more robust and practical defense mechanisms.

</details>


### [171] [Trans-RAG: Query-Centric Vector Transformation for Secure Cross-Organizational Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09541)
*Yu Liu,Kun Peng,Wenxiao Zhang,Fangfang Yuan,Cong Cao,Wenxuan Lu,Yanbing Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: Trans-RAG提出了一种新的向量空间语言范式，通过向量转换技术实现跨组织RAG系统的安全高效检索，避免了传统加密方法的解密开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨组织部署的RAG系统面临安全、准确性和效率之间的根本矛盾。现有加密方法在解密时暴露明文，而联邦架构又阻碍资源整合且开销巨大。

Method: 引入Trans-RAG系统，采用向量空间语言范式，每个组织的知识存在于数学隔离的语义空间中。核心是vector2Trans多阶段转换技术，使查询能够通过查询中心转换动态"说"每个组织的向量空间"语言"。

Result: 安全评估显示近乎正交的向量空间（89.90°角度分离）和99.81%的隔离率。在8个检索器、3个数据集和3个LLM上的实验显示准确性下降最小（nDCG@10下降3.5%），相比同态加密有显著效率提升。

Conclusion: Trans-RAG通过创新的向量空间语言范式解决了跨组织RAG系统的安全-效率权衡问题，在保持高安全性的同时实现了接近原生检索的效率。

Abstract: Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) systems deployed across organizational boundaries face fundamental tensions between security, accuracy, and efficiency. Current encryption methods expose plaintext during decryption, while federated architectures prevent resource integration and incur substantial overhead. We introduce Trans-RAG, implementing a novel vector space language paradigm where each organization's knowledge exists in a mathematically isolated semantic space. At the core lies vector2Trans, a multi-stage transformation technique that enables queries to dynamically "speak" each organization's vector space "language" through query-centric transformations, eliminating decryption overhead while maintaining native retrieval efficiency. Security evaluations demonstrate near-orthogonal vector spaces with 89.90° angular separation and 99.81% isolation rates. Experiments across 8 retrievers, 3 datasets, and 3 LLMs show minimal accuracy degradation (3.5% decrease in nDCG@10) and significant efficiency improvements over homomorphic encryption.

</details>

### [172] [Systematic API Testing Through Model Checking and Executable Contracts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08633)
*Ana Ribeiro,Margarida Mamede,Carla Ferreira*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: IcePick框架通过模型检查实现API系统化状态空间覆盖，结合Glacier契约语言解决语义验证问题，在EvoMaster基准测试中证明能实现完整状态覆盖并发现多操作交互故障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统API黑盒测试依赖接口规范但缺乏行为语义，导致测试预言问题和状态化调用序列生成受限，需要系统化的状态空间覆盖方法。

Method: 使用TLA+形式化建模API状态演化，利用TLC模型检查器穷举可达状态，采用覆盖引导的广度优先遍历缓解状态空间爆炸，提出Glacier一阶逻辑契约语言增强语义验证。

Result: 在EvoMaster基准系统评估中，模型检查引导的探索实现了完整状态覆盖，揭示了多操作交互中的故障，分析了可扩展性和实际应用限制。

Conclusion: IcePick为关键API系统提供了具有强覆盖保证的可重复测试套件，通过形式化建模和模型检查解决了API测试中的语义覆盖问题。

Abstract: Automated black-box testing of APIs typically relies on interface specifications that define available operations and data schemas, but offer limited or no behavioural semantics. This semantic gap amplifies the test-oracle problem and limits the generation of effective, stateful call sequences.
  We introduce IcePick, a framework that achieves systematic state-space coverage for API testing by leveraging model checking. IcePick uses TLA+ to formally model API state evolution, employs the TLC model checker to exhaustively explore reachable states, and generates test sequences that provably cover the behavioural model. To mitigate state-space explosion and improve sequence extraction, we introduce a coverage-guided breadth-first traversal of the TLC state-space graph. To address oracle limitations beyond HTTP status codes, we propose Glacier, a first-order logic contract language that enriches API specifications with executable semantic contracts, enabling automated behavioural verification during test execution.
  We evaluate IcePick on EvoMaster Benchmark systems, demonstrating that model-checking-guided exploration achieves complete state coverage and reveals faults in multi-operation interactions. We also analyse scalability to characterise practical limits and applicability requirements. Overall, IcePick provides reproducible test suites with strong coverage guarantees for critical API-based systems.

### [173] [An Eye for Trust: An Exploration of Developers' Trust Perceptions Through Urgency and Reputation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08713)
*Sara Yabesi,Mahta Amini,Jelena Ristic,Zohreh Sharafi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究通过眼动追踪实验发现，代码优先级（紧迫性）和作者经验（声誉）会影响开发者的代码审查行为，包括评估时间、认知负荷和感知质量，但不会影响最终的代码采纳决策。参与者主要关注代码功能、质量和可理解性，却忽视了紧迫性和声誉对其决策的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码重用是软件开发中的普遍实践，但缺乏对开发者信任机制的基本理解。研究旨在探索紧迫性（代码优先级）和声誉（作者经验水平）如何影响开发者对代码可信度的认知过程。

Method: 采用第一个受控眼动追踪实验（n=37），通过代码优先级代表紧迫性，作者经验水平代表声誉，研究这些因素如何影响开发者对代码可信度的感知。

Result: 1. 代码优先级显著影响代码审查行为（评估时间、认知负荷、感知质量），但不影响代码采纳决策；2. 眼动数据显示，对标注为资深vs初级开发者编写的相同代码，视觉扫描模式和注意力分布存在差异，但性能无显著差异；3. 参与者主要关注代码功能、质量和可理解性；4. 参与者忽视了紧迫性和声誉对其审查和重用决策的实质性影响。

Conclusion: 尽管代码审查行为有明显变化，但开发者低估了紧迫性和声誉对其决策的影响。该研究为理解软件工程中的信任机制迈出了重要一步，可为代码审查平台、代码重用和自动代码生成的研究提供参考。

Abstract: Code reuse is a widespread practice across software development projects, suggesting an inherent trust in the reused code. Yet, there is a lack of a fundamental understanding of developers' trust and how various factors mold their trust-based cognitive processes. Drawing from the psychology of compliance and trust, we present the results of the first controlled experiment (n=37) which uses eye tracking to explore how urgency (represented by code priority level) and reputation (represented by the experience level of the code's author) influence developers' perceptions of code trustworthiness.
  Our research revealed that the priority assigned to a code patch significantly influenced developers' code review behavior, impacting their evaluation time, cognitive load, and perceived quality. However, the decision to incorporate and implement the code was not affected . Eye tracking data revealed that there were variations in overall visual code scanning and the distribution of attention across identical code patches labeled as written by senior vs. junior developers. Yet, there were no significant performance differences. Moreover, our participants nominate code functionality, quality, and comprehensibility as primary factors in code evaluation.
  Despite noticeable changes in code review behavior, our participants surprisingly overlooked the substantial influence of urgency and reputation on their decisions to review and reuse code changes. This study takes the next step toward a better understanding of trust in software engineering and may inform future research about code review platforms and guidelines, code reuse, and automated code generation.

</details>


### [174] [Demystifying the Silence of Correctness Bugs in PyTorch Compiler](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08720)
*Meiziniu Li,Dongze Li,Jianmeng Liu,Shing-Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次对PyTorch编译器(torch.compile)的正确性bug进行实证研究，分析了这些bug的特征，并提出了专门检测此类bug的测试技术AlignGuard。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: torch.compile作为深度学习模型（包括大语言模型）的核心优化工具，存在导致编译后模型输出错误而不触发异常、崩溃或警告的正确性bug。这些bug严重威胁下游LLM应用的可靠性，但尚未有系统研究专门针对这些bug进行特征分析和检测。

Method: 首先对torch.compile的正确性bug进行实证研究，分析其特征并评估现有模糊测试工具的效果。基于研究发现，提出了专门检测torch.compile正确性bug的测试技术AlignGuard，该技术结合了从实证研究中提炼的bug特征，并应用基于LLM的测试变异来增强现有测试用例的检测能力。

Result: AlignGuard成功检测到23个torch.compile中的新正确性bug，所有bug均被PyTorch开发团队确认或修复，其中超过一半（14/23）被标记为高优先级bug，证明了该技术的有效性。

Conclusion: torch.compile的正确性bug是一个严重但被忽视的问题，需要专门的检测方法。AlignGuard通过结合实证研究发现的bug特征和LLM-based测试变异，能够有效检测这类bug，为PyTorch编译器的可靠性提供了重要保障。

Abstract: Performance optimization of AI infrastructure is key to the fast adoption of large language models (LLMs). The PyTorch compiler (torch.compile), a core optimization tool for deep learning (DL) models (including LLMs), has received due attention. However, torch.compile is prone to correctness bugs, which cause incorrect outputs of compiled DL models without triggering exceptions, crashes, or warnings. These bugs pose a serious threat to the reliability of downstream LLM applications. Data from the PyTorch community shows that 19.2% of high-priority issues are incorrect outputs of compiled DL models induced by torch.compile bugs, the second-most-common bug category (only behind program crashes at 19.57%). However, no systematic study has been conducted to specifically characterize and thereby detect these bugs. In this paper, we present the first empirical study of the correctness bugs in torch.compile, examine their characteristics, and assess the effectiveness of existing fuzzers in detecting them. Based on our findings, we propose a proof-of-concept testing technique named AlignGuard, tailored specifically for detecting correctness bugs in torch.compile. AlignGuard incorporates bug characteristics distilled from our empirical study, applying LLM-based test mutation to existing test cases for correctness bug detection. At the time of writing, AlignGuard has successfully detected 23 new correctness bugs in recent torch.compile. All these bugs have been confirmed or fixed by the PyTorch development team, and over half (14/23) of them are even marked as high-priority bugs, underscoring the usefulness of our technique.

</details>


### [175] [A Longitudinal Study of Dependency Reclassifications in JavaScript Projects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08747)
*Yuxin Liu,Cristian Bogdan,Benoit Baudry*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究JavaScript项目中依赖项重新分类的普遍性、类型和模式，发现依赖项重新分类是普遍存在的维护活动，涉及依赖项移除和角色重新分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注依赖项版本更新，但对开发者如何随时间调整依赖项角色（如运行时依赖、开发依赖、对等依赖）了解不足。本研究旨在探索JavaScript项目中依赖项重新分类的实践模式。

Method: 分析33,087个活跃维护的JavaScript项目，研究依赖项重新分类活动，包括依赖项移除和角色重新分配（Core/Dev/Peer角色）。

Result: 79.1%的项目存在依赖项重新分类；97.2%的项目会移除依赖项；38.0%的项目进行角色重新分配；33.1%的项目会重新引入已移除的依赖项；11.2%的项目存在重复角色切换；重新分类活动持续时间中位数为408天。

Conclusion: 依赖项重新分类是JavaScript项目中普遍且长期存在的维护活动，超越了传统的版本更新研究，对依赖项工具、包管理器和研究有重要启示。

Abstract: Modern software projects depend on third-party dependencies, whose declarations must be maintained as projects evolve. Prior work has focused on dependency version updates, while much less is known about how developers assign dependencies to different roles over time. In this paper, we investigate how developers of JavaScript projects reclassify their dependencies, including removal and role reassignment. Our analysis of 33,087 JavaScript projects with active dependency maintenance reveals that dependency reclassification is a prevalent maintenance activity, occurring in 79.1% of the studied projects. Of these projects, nearly all (97.2%) remove dependencies at some point, while 38.0% undergo role reassignments across Core (runtime), Dev (development-only), and Peer (consumer-provided) roles. These changes are not always final, as 33.1% of projects later reintroduce removed dependencies and 11.2% exhibit repeated role switching. Reclassification practices also tend to unfold over long periods, with a median duration of 408 days. These findings broaden the study of dependency maintenance beyond version updates, and contribute implications for dependency tools, package managers, and research to support correct dependency role declarations.

Abstract: Toxic interactions in open-source software development harm community collaboration. We bridge the gap by conducting a comprehensive study of 409 fixed bugs from five representative agentic frameworks. ### [178] [DeepGuard: Secure Code Generation via Multi-Layer Semantic Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09089)
*Li Huang,Zhongxin Liu,Yifan Wu,Tao Yin,Dong Li,Jichao Bi,Nankun Mu,Hongyu Zhang,Meng Yan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DeepGuard通过聚合多个上层表征来增强代码LLM的安全性，解决了最终层瓶颈问题，在保持功能正确性的同时平均提升11.9%的安全正确生成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码生成LLM会复制训练数据中的不安全模式。现有安全加固方法通常基于最终层监督进行微调，但存在"最终层瓶颈"问题：漏洞判别线索可能分布在多个层中，在专注于下一词预测的输出表征中变得难以检测。

Method: 通过层间线性探测发现漏洞相关信号在中间到上层最明显，但在最终层衰减。基于此，提出DeepGuard框架：1) 使用注意力模块聚合多个上层表征；2) 通过多目标训练平衡安全增强和功能正确性；3) 支持轻量级推理时引导策略。

Result: 在五个代码LLM上的实验表明，DeepGuard相比SVEN等强基线平均提升11.9%的安全正确生成率，保持功能正确性，并能泛化到未见过的漏洞类型。

Conclusion: DeepGuard通过利用分布式安全相关线索有效缓解了最终层瓶颈问题，显著提升了代码LLM的安全生成能力，同时保持了功能正确性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) for code generation can replicate insecure patterns from their training data. To mitigate this, a common strategy for security hardening is to fine-tune models using supervision derived from the final transformer layer. However, this design may suffer from a final-layer bottleneck: vulnerability-discriminative cues can be distributed across layers and become less detectable near the output representations optimized for next-token prediction. To diagnose this issue, we perform layer-wise linear probing. We observe that vulnerability-related signals are most detectable in a band of intermediate-to-upper layers yet attenuate toward the final layers. Motivated by this observation, we introduce DeepGuard, a framework that leverages distributed security-relevant cues by aggregating representations from multiple upper layers via an attention-based module. The aggregated signal powers a dedicated security analyzer within a multi-objective training objective that balances security enhancement and functional correctness, and further supports a lightweight inference-time steering strategy. Extensive experiments across five code LLMs demonstrate that DeepGuard improves the secure-and-correct generation rate by an average of 11.9% over strong baselines such as SVEN. It also preserves functional correctness while exhibiting generalization to held-out vulnerability types. Our code is public at https://github.com/unknownhl/DeepGuard.

### [179] [The Role of LLMs in Collaborative Software Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09120)
*Victoria Jackson,Yoonha Cha,Rafael Prikladnicki,André van der Hoek*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究探索大型语言模型如何影响软件工程中的协作设计工作，发现LLM引入导致不同的使用模式，从共享实例促进共同理解到并行使用导致"上下文漂移"，专业人员对LLM输出的审查和反思常产生设计洞见，但早期锚定可能限制探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已有大量研究关注大型语言模型在独立开发任务中的应用，但关于LLM如何影响软件工程中协作团队工作的了解还很少。本研究聚焦于软件设计这一协作任务，探索LLM在专业软件团队中的实际使用情况。

Method: 对18对软件专业人员进行探索性实验室研究，让他们自由使用LLM设计大学校园自行车停车应用。研究人员观察他们如何使用LLM以及LLM如何影响协作设计过程。

Result: 研究发现LLM引入导致不同的联合使用模式：共享实例使用促进共同理解，而跨单独实例的并行使用有时导致"上下文漂移"。专业人员对LLM的依赖程度差异很大，从完全不使用到将其视为信息源或生产者。专业人员会仔细审查和反思LLM的响应，这常产生设计洞见，但早期锚定有时会限制探索。

Conclusion: 研究为设计工具提供了启示，这些工具可以在保持设计以人为中心的同时辅助设计师。需要开发能够支持协作设计过程而不损害人类创造性和探索性的LLM集成工具。

Abstract: While much prior work examines Large Language Models (LLMs) for solo development tasks (e.g., coding), far less is known about how LLMs shape collaborative group work in software engineering. This study focuses on one such collaborative task, namely software design. It presents the results of an exploratory laboratory study of 18 pairs of software professionals who could use an LLM however they saw fit, to design a University campus bicycle parking application. Our findings reveal that introducing an LLM leads to distinct patterns of joint use: shared-instance use facilitated shared understanding, whereas parallel use across separate instances sometimes led to ''context drift''. We also observe wide variation in reliance, from non-use to treating the LLM as an information source or producer. Across these modes, professionals scrutinized and reflected on LLM responses, often yielding design insights; however, early anchoring sometimes curtailed exploration. We provide implications for tools to aid designers while retaining the human-centricity important to design.

To address this bottleneck, we propose SHIFT (Sigmoid-Based Heuristic Invertible Fitness-Landscape Transformation for Accelerating SBST), a method designed to compress local landscapes and facilitate escape from stagnant regions without altering global semantics. By systematically contracting dense regions where search points cluster, the approach preserves mapping invertibility while enabling optimization algorithms to traverse more effectively toward global coverage with the same step size. When evaluated against established baselines, including pure hill climbing and genetic algorithms, under a normalized experimental protocol, the proposed technique yields consistent improvements in convergence speed and search efficiency. ### [183] [LLM-Rosetta: A Hub-and-Spoke Intermediate Representation for Cross-Provider LLM API Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09360)
*Peng Ding*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LLM-Rosetta是一个开源翻译框架，通过中心辐射型中间表示解决LLM API碎片化问题，实现不同提供商API之间的双向转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型提供商众多且API格式各异，导致应用程序与特定供应商紧密耦合。切换或桥接不同提供商需要O(N²)的双边适配器，阻碍了可移植性和多提供商架构的发展。

Method: 基于观察发现主要LLM API具有共同的语义核心，设计了一个中心辐射型中间表示，包含9类型内容模型和10类型流事件模式。采用模块化Ops组合转换器架构，每个API标准可独立添加，支持请求和响应负载的双向转换，包括带状态上下文管理的分块流处理。

Result: 实现了对四种主流API标准（OpenAI Chat Completions、OpenAI Responses、Anthropic Messages、Google GenAI）的转换器，覆盖大多数商业提供商。实证评估显示无损往返保真度、正确的流行为，以及低于100微秒的转换开销，与LiteLLM的单向方法竞争性相当，同时提供双向性和提供商中立性。

Conclusion: LLM-Rosetta成功解决了LLM API碎片化问题，通过了Open Responses合规套件测试，并在阿贡国家实验室投入生产使用，为多提供商LLM应用提供了有效的标准化解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of Large Language Model (LLM) providers--each exposing proprietary API formats--has created a fragmented ecosystem where applications become tightly coupled to individual vendors. Switching or bridging providers requires $O(N^2)$ bilateral adapters, impeding portability and multi-provider architectures. We observe that despite substantial syntactic divergence, the major LLM APIs share a common semantic core: the practical challenge is the combinatorial surface of syntactic variations, not deep semantic incompatibility. Based on this finding, we present LLM-Rosetta, an open-source translation framework built on a hub-and-spoke Intermediate Representation (IR) that captures the shared semantic core--messages, content parts, tool calls, reasoning traces, and generation controls--in a 9-type content model and 10-type stream event schema. A modular Ops-composition converter architecture enables each API standard to be added independently. LLM-Rosetta supports bidirectional conversion (provider-to-IR-to-provider) for both request and response payloads, including chunk-level streaming with stateful context management. We implement converters for four API standards (OpenAI Chat Completions, OpenAI Responses, Anthropic Messages, and Google GenAI), covering the vast majority of commercial providers. Empirical evaluation demonstrates lossless round-trip fidelity, correct streaming behavior, and sub-100 microsecond conversion overhead--competitive with LiteLLM's single-pass approach while providing bidirectionality and provider neutrality. LLM-Rosetta passes the Open Responses compliance suite and is deployed in production at Argonne National Laboratory. Code is available at https://github.com/Oaklight/llm-rosetta.

</details>


### [184] [The AI Codebase Maturity Model: From Assisted Coding to Self-Sustaining Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09388)
*Andy Anderson*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了AI代码库成熟度模型（ACMM），这是一个5级框架，描述代码库如何从基本的AI辅助编码演变为自持系统。通过4个月构建KubeStellar Console的经验验证，发现AI驱动开发系统的智能不在于AI模型本身，而在于围绕它的指令、测试、指标和反馈循环基础设施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI编码工具被广泛采用，但大多数团队停留在"提示-审查"阶段，缺乏系统化进展的框架。需要一种方法来指导团队如何从基本的AI辅助编码逐步发展到更成熟的AI驱动开发系统。

Method: 提出了AI代码库成熟度模型（ACMM），这是一个受CMMI启发的5级框架，每个级别由其反馈循环拓扑定义。通过4个月维护KubeStellar Console（使用Claude Code和GitHub Copilot构建的CNCF Kubernetes仪表板）的经验报告来验证模型。

Result: 系统运行良好：拥有63个CI/CD工作流，32个夜间测试套件，91%的代码覆盖率，bug修复时间在30分钟内，全天候运行。核心发现：AI驱动开发系统的智能不在于AI模型本身，而在于围绕它的基础设施。测试（测试用例数量、覆盖率阈值和测试执行可靠性）是整个旅程中最重要的投资。

Conclusion: AI代码库成熟度模型为团队提供了系统化进展的框架。关键见解是：无法跳过级别，每个级别解锁下一个级别的都是另一个反馈机制。测试基础设施的建立是实现高级别成熟度的最关键因素。

Abstract: AI coding tools are widely adopted, but most teams plateau at prompt-and-review without a framework for systematic progression. This paper presents the AI Codebase Maturity Model (ACMM), a 5-level framework describing how codebases evolve from basic AI-assisted coding to self-sustaining systems. Inspired by CMMI, each level is defined by its feedback loop topology the specific mechanisms that must exist before the next level becomes possible. I validate the model through a 4-month experience report maintaining KubeStellar Console, a CNCF Kubernetes dashboard built from scratch with Claude Code (Opus) and GitHub Copilot. The system currently operates with 63 CI/CD workflows, 32 nightly test suites, 91% code coverage, and achieves bug-to-fix times under 30 minutes 24 hours a day. The central finding: the intelligence of an AI-driven development system resides not in the AI model itself, but in the infrastructure of instructions, tests, metrics, and feedback loops that surround it. You cannot skip levels, and at each level, the thing that unlocks the next one is another feedback mechanism. Testing the volume of test cases, the coverage thresholds, and the reliability of test execution proved to be the single most important investment in the entire journey.

</details>


### [185] [When LLMs Lag Behind: Knowledge Conflicts from Evolving APIs in Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09515)
*Ahmed Nusayer Ashik,Shaowei Wang,Tse-Hsun Chen,Muhammad Asaduzzaman,Yuan Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文研究了大型语言模型在软件库API演化（如弃用、修改、新增）时的代码生成能力，发现即使提供最新API文档，模型仍难以优先使用外部上下文，导致生成代码可执行率低（平均42.55%），结构化文档和更大模型规模仅部分改善（66.36%），而推理策略（如自我反思）能显著提升性能（11%改进）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件库的快速演化给大型语言模型带来挑战，因为模型的静态参数知识在训练后容易过时。虽然检索增强生成常用于提供最新的API规范，但当外部指令与模型内部参数知识冲突时会出现"上下文-记忆冲突"。需要系统研究LLM在API演化下的代码生成能力。

Method: 构建包含8个Python库中270个真实更新的基准测试，评估4个LLM家族的11个模型。研究API弃用、修改和新增三种演化类型，分析模型在有无全面文档、不同模型规模、以及使用推理策略（如自我反思）时的表现。

Result: 在没有全面文档时，LLM难以优先使用外部上下文，平均只有42.55%的生成代码示例在目标环境中可执行。结构化文档和更大模型规模能改善更新采用，但可执行率仍较低（66.36%）。推理策略显著提升性能，可执行率提高11%。

Conclusion: 即使提供API更新规范，LLM仍会坚持使用过时的模式，凸显了演化感知基准测试和技术的必要性。需要开发能更好处理API演化的技术，以解决LLM在动态软件环境中的实际应用问题。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of software libraries creates a significant challenge for Large Language Models (LLMs), whose static parametric knowledge often becomes stale post-training. While retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is commonly used to provide up-to-date API specifications, "context-memory conflict" arises when external instructions contradict a model's internal parametric knowledge. This paper presents a systematic empirical study of LLM code generation under API evolution (e.g., API deprecation, API modification, and API addition), by constructing a benchmark of 270 real-world updates from eight Python libraries. We evaluate four LLM families of 11 models. Our results show that without comprehensive documentation, LLMs struggle to prioritize external context, averaging only 42.55% of generated code examples are executable in the target environment. While structured documentation and larger model scales improve LLMs' ability to update adoption, they do not fully resolve executability issues with a low 66.36% executable rate. In addition, reasoning-based strategies (e.g., Self-Reflection) significantly boost LLMs' performance with 11% improvement on executable rate. Our findings highlight the persistence of outdated patterns from LLMs, even when API update specifications are provided, and emphasize the need for evolution-aware benchmarks and techniques.

</details>

### [186] [Beyond the Individual: Virtualizing Multi-Disciplinary Reasoning for Clinical Intake via Collaborative Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08927)
*Huangwei Chen,Wu Li,Junhao Jia,Yining Chen,Xiaotao Pang,Ya-Long Chen,Li Gonghui,Haishuai Wang,Jiajun Bu,Lei Wu*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: Aegle是一个基于图的多智能体虚拟多学科团队框架，旨在通过同步虚拟MDT提升门诊咨询质量，减少认知偏差，在文档质量和诊断准确性方面优于现有模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统门诊咨询通常由单一医生在时间压力下完成，容易产生认知偏差和证据收集不完整的问题。虽然多学科团队（MDT）能减少这些风险，但成本高昂且难以实时扩展。

Method: 提出Aegle同步虚拟MDT框架，采用基于图的多智能体架构，使用结构化SOAP表示形式化咨询状态，将证据收集与诊断推理分离。通过协调器动态激活专科智能体进行解耦并行推理，最后由聚合器整合为连贯的临床记录。

Result: 在ClinicalBench和真实世界RAPID-IPN数据集上的实验表明，Aegle在24个科室和53个指标上持续优于最先进的专有和开源模型，在文档质量和咨询能力方面表现更优，同时提高了最终诊断准确性。

Conclusion: Aegle框架成功将MDT级推理引入门诊咨询，通过虚拟多学科团队架构有效解决了传统咨询中的认知偏差问题，为实时、可扩展的高质量临床决策提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The initial outpatient consultation is critical for clinical decision-making, yet it is often conducted by a single physician under time pressure, making it prone to cognitive biases and incomplete evidence capture. Although the Multi-Disciplinary Team (MDT) reduces these risks, they are costly and difficult to scale to real-time intake. We propose Aegle, a synchronous virtual MDT framework that brings MDT-level reasoning to outpatient consultations via a graph-based multi-agent architecture. Aegle formalizes the consultation state using a structured SOAP representation, separating evidence collection from diagnostic reasoning to improve traceability and bias control. An orchestrator dynamically activates specialist agents, which perform decoupled parallel reasoning and are subsequently integrated by an aggregator into a coherent clinical note. Experiments on ClinicalBench and a real-world RAPID-IPN dataset across 24 departments and 53 metrics show that Aegle consistently outperforms state-of-the-art proprietary and open-source models in documentation quality and consultation capability, while also improving final diagnosis accuracy. Our code is available at https://github.com/HovChen/Aegle.

</details>


### [187] [Aligned Agents, Biased Swarm: Measuring Bias Amplification in Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08963)
*Keyu Li,Jin Gao,Dequan Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 研究发现多智能体系统的结构复杂性不仅不能保证伦理鲁棒性，反而可能放大偏见，形成系统性极化


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统在复杂工作流中部署日益增多，但其涌现特性特别是偏见积累机制尚不明确。由于现实MAS过于复杂难以全面分析，需要先研究其基础机制来评估伦理鲁棒性。

Method: 引入Discrim-Eval-Open开放基准，通过强制跨人口群体比较判断绕过个体模型中立性；分析不同MAS拓扑结构和反馈环对偏见的影响；研究基础动态而非高级群体复杂性。

Result: 发现架构复杂性常加剧而非缓解偏见；即使孤立智能体中立运行，仍出现系统性偏见放大；识别出"触发脆弱性"现象，纯客观上下文注入会急剧加速极化。

Conclusion: 结构复杂性不能保证伦理鲁棒性，结构化工作流可能成为回音室，将微小随机偏见放大为系统性极化，为MAS伦理评估建立了重要基准。

Abstract: While Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) are increasingly deployed for complex workflows, their emergent properties-particularly the accumulation of bias-remain poorly understood. Because real-world MAS are too complex to analyze entirely, evaluating their ethical robustness requires first isolating their foundational mechanics. In this work, we conduct a baseline empirical study investigating how basic MAS topologies and feedback loops influence prejudice. Contrary to the assumption that multi-agent collaboration naturally dilutes bias, we hypothesize that structured workflows act as echo chambers, amplifying minor stochastic biases into systemic polarization. To evaluate this, we introduce Discrim-Eval-Open, an open-ended benchmark that bypasses individual model neutrality through forced comparative judgments across demographic groups. Analyzing bias cascades across various structures reveals that architectural sophistication frequently exacerbates bias rather than mitigating it. We observe systemic amplification even when isolated agents operate neutrally, and identify a 'Trigger Vulnerability' where injecting purely objective context drastically accelerates polarization. By stripping away advanced swarm complexity to study foundational dynamics, we establish a crucial baseline: structural complexity does not guarantee ethical robustness. Our code is available at https://github.com/weizhihao1/MAS-Bias.

</details>


### [188] [Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning for Low-Carbon P2P Energy Trading among Self-Interested Microgrids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08973)
*Junhao Ren,Honglin Gao,Lan Zhao,Qiyu Kang,Gaoxi Xiao,Yajuan Sun*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 提出多智能体强化学习框架，让自利的微电网参与P2P电力交易，通过储能套利优化自身利润，同时提高可再生能源利用率并减少高碳电力依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可再生能源发电和需求动态的不确定性给日前调度带来挑战，需要提高可再生能源渗透率并维持日内平衡。

Method: 开发多智能体强化学习框架，每个微电网独立进行价格和数量投标，在时变主网电价下通过储能套利优化自身利润，并提出协调交易并促进激励相容的市场出清机制。

Result: 仿真结果显示，学习到的投标策略提高了可再生能源利用率，减少了对高碳电力的依赖，同时增加了社区层面的经济福利，实现了减排和地方繁荣的双赢。

Conclusion: 该多智能体强化学习框架为自利微电网参与P2P电力交易提供了有效解决方案，能够在提高可再生能源利用的同时实现经济和环境效益的双赢。

Abstract: Uncertainties in renewable generation and demand dynamics challenge day-ahead scheduling. To enhance renewable penetration and maintain intra-day balance, we develop a multi-agent reinforcement learning framework for self-interested microgrids participating in peer-to-peer (P2P) electricity trading. Each microgrid independently bids both price and quantity while optimizing its own profit via storage arbitrage under time-varying main-grid prices. A market-clearing mechanism coordinating trades and promoting incentive compatibility is proposed. Simulation results show that the learned bidding policy improves renewable utilization and reduces reliance on high-carbon electricity, while increasing community-level economic welfare, delivering a win-win situation in emission reduction and local prosperity.

</details>
